 " Kamada Ekadashi 2019: Kamada Ekadashi is the day of attaining the grace of Lord Vishnu
 kaamada ekadshi kaa vrath bada hi divya or chamatkaari mana jaataa he
 On this day, the worship of Vasudev Shri Krishna with Lord Vishnu destroys all worldly faults and sins
 manyata he ki jo insaan is vrath ko puri vidhi se kar letaa he, uske saare paap swayan hi nasht ho jate hai
 Let's know why this Ekadashi is so important
 kaamada ekadshi kaa mahatv-- sharir or man ko santulit karne ke liye vrath or upwas ke niyam banaae gaye hai
 Ekadashi is the most important of all the fasts and fasts
 - ekadshi maheene main do baar padati hai
 One in Shukla Paksha and the other in Krishna Paksha
 - ekadshi vrath main mukhya rup se bhagwaan vishnu, bhagwaan krishna yaa unke avtaron kii puja hoti he
 - Ekadashi fasting has special significance in Chaitra month
 - kaamada ekadshi se man or sharir donon hi santulit rahete hai, rogon se raksha hoti he
 Kamada Ekadashi has special significance for the destruction of sins and fulfillment of desires
 agar ekadshi kaa vrath nahin rakh paaen to ye upaay karen-- snaan ke baad bhagwaan vishnu yaa shrikrishna kii puja karen
 - Be sattvic and keep the mind pure
 - is din ann or baari bhojan khaane se parhez karen
 - Devote more and more time to the worship of God
 kaamada ekadshi par vasudev krishna kii upasna kaa bhi vidhaan he
 By worshiping Shri Krishna on this day, a person can get rid of all his sins
 aaie jaanate hai kaamada ekadshi par kaise karen bhagwaan krishna kii puja-upasna-kaamada ekadshi puja-upasna-- is din subah nahaakar pehle surya ko arghya den
 Then worship Lord Krishna
 - kanha ko pile phool, fal, panchamrita or tulsi dal arpit karen
 After this, meditate on Lord Krishna and chant his mantras
 - is din puri tarah jaleey aahaar yaa falahar len to is vrath ke uttam parinaam milenge
 - If you keep only one Vela, then take Vaishnav food in the other Vela
 - agle din subah kisi nirdhan ko ek vela kaa bhojan yaa ann daan karen
 - Put your mind in God on this day
 krodh naa karen or jhooth naa bolen
 Great Measures of Sin Destruction - Offer a garland of sandalwood to Lord Krishna
 - iske baad "clin krishna clin" kaa 11 maala jaap karen
 - Keep the garland of sandalwood offered to you
 - aapke naam or yash main vruddhi hogi
 One will get the blessing of children from Ekadashi fast - husband and wife jointly offer yellow fruits and yellow flowers to Lord Krishna
 - ek saath santan gopal mantra kaa kam se kam 11 maala jaap karen
 - Then pray to have children
 - fal ko pati-patni prasad ke rup main grahan karen

 The history of phone tapping in Indian politics is quite old

 )phone tanping par bavaal machaa hua he

 Phone tapping started in the era of Prime Minister Jawaharlal Nehru
 us samay yah aarope lagane vaale koi or nahin khud sanchaar mantri rafee ahamed kidawai thea
 He made this charge against the then Home Minister Sardar Patel, which he did not listen to
 phone tanping kaa itihaas:-1959: sena pramukh general kees thimaya ne apane or army offis ke phone tepe hone kaa aarope lagaaya tha
 1962: Another minister of the Nehru government, TT Krishnamachari, accused the phone of being tapped
 1988: apane raajnneetik virodhiyon ke phone tepe karwaane ke aarope main karnataka ke mukhyamantri ramakrishna hegade ko kursi chhodana padi thi
 1991: The then Prime Minister Chandrasekhar was accused of tapping the phone, after which he had to wash his hands from his chair
 1996: indian telegraph act 1885 main centre or rajya sarkaron ko is baat ke adhikaar die gaye hai ki wo janhit main yaa immergency main massej intercept kar sakati he, lekin 1996 main supreme court ne is par disha-nirdesh dete hue kaha tha ki avaidh tareeke se phone tanping gambhir maamla he or iske aadesh grih sachiv str par milane chahie or wo bhi kuch nirdhaarit samay ke liye
 2004-2006: Between June 2004 to March 2006, over 40 thousand phones were taped by government agencies
 2006: amar singh ke phone tanping ko lekar bhi bavaal hua tha lekin supreme court ne use jari karne par roak laga di

 Etah, the birthplace of the great Sufi saint Amir Khusro, is considered very important from the political perspective of Uttar Pradesh
 eta sansadeey seat uttar pradesh ke charchit loksabhaa siton main shumaar kii jaati he or pichhali baar kii tarah is baar bhi is seat par sabhi kii najar rahegi kyonki purv mukhyamantri kalyaan singh ke bete rajvir singh maidan main hai or un par chunaav main jeet hasil karne kaa dabaav he jabaki unke khilaaf is baar sapa-basapa kii jodi he
 There are 14 candidates in the fray for the Etah parliamentary seat, in which the main contest is between Rajveer Singh alias Raju Bhaiya of Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP) and Devendra Singh Yadav of Samajwadi Party
 is seat par congress ne apana ummidavaar khadaa nahin kiya he
 The Congress has tied up with 3 regional parties in UP
 isi gathbandhan ke tahat congress ne yah seat rashtriya jan adhikaar party (arajeepi) ke liye chodi he or arajeepi ne suraj singh ko maidan main utaara he
 Apart from 8 regional parties and 5 independent candidates are in the fray
 kanpur or fatehpur sikri loksabhaa seat se sate eta main pehla chunaav (1952) congress ne jeeta tha, lekin uske baad yahaan se hindu mahasabha ne pehle 1957 phir 1962 main jeet darj kii
 However, after that the Congress came back strongly by winning the general elections of 1967 and 1971
 1977 main chali congress virdohi lahar main choudhary charan singh kii bhartiya lokdal ne bade antar se jeet darj kii thi
 The Congress last won from here in the 1980 election
 1984 main bhartiya lok dal ke jeet darj karne ke baad yah seat bhartiya janata party (bijepi) ke khate main aa gai
 Here in 1989, 1991, 1996 and 1998, Mahakdeep Singh Shakya of Bharatiya Janata Party won by a big margin
 1999 or 2004 eta se lagaataar do baar samaajawaadee party kaa paracham laharaaya
 In the 2009 Lok Sabha elections, former Chief Minister Kalyan Singh broke away from the Bharatiya Janata Party and formed his own party and won the election
 2014 ke chunaav main kalyaan singh ke bete rajvir singh ko tikat mila or unhone badi jeet hasil kii
 The Etah parliamentary constituency is very important in terms of the 2014 mandate of the ethnic equation
 eta kshetra main lodh, yadav or shakya bahul jatiyaan rahati hai
 In the last Lok Sabha election, this seat had around 16 lakh voters, out of which 8
 5 lakh purush or 7
 There are 2 lakh women voters
 eta loksabhaa kshetra main kul 5 vidhansabha siten aati hai, inamen kasganj, amopur, patiyaali, eta or marhara vidhansabha siten shaamil hai
 In 2014, the Modi wave in the country also benefited in Etah and the Bharatiya Janata Party directly defeated the Samajwadi Party
 eta main hue 58 fisadi matdaan main bijepi ke rajvir singh ko kareeb 51 fisadi vot mili to unke pratidwandvi samaajawaadee party ke ummidavaar ko sirf 29 fisadi vot mili the

 maweshiyon kii kharid-farokht ke sambandh main centre sarkaar ke nae notification par madras hoicourt ne chaar hafte ke liye roak laga di he
 The Central Government, through this notification, announced a ban on the slaughter of cattle sold in cattle markets
 madras hoicourt kii madurai bench ne centre or rajya sarkaar se is maamle par ek maheene ke bheetar jawaab daayar karne ko kaha he
 The court issued this order while hearing a PIL filed in this regard
 janhit yachika main mukhya rup se do muddon ko uthaaya gaya he
 First- the latest notification of the central government is an attack on people's freedom to eat and drink and second- to stop the buying and selling of animals is an interference in business and profession
 bataa den ki hoicourt kaa yah faisla aise samay main aayaa he, jab centre sarkaar ke is faisle ko lekar virodh badhata ja rahaa he
 The Chief Ministers of Kerala and West Bengal have said to challenge the government's decision in the court, saying that the Center is violating the rights of the states
 centre sarkaar ke faisle ke virodh main kerala, tamilnadu or karnataka main pradarshan bhi hue hai
 The comments pashu bazaar main vadh ke liye pashuon kii bikri par roak lagaae jane ko lekar centre par barasate hue kerala ke mukhyamantri pi
 Vijayan had said on Sunday that the people of his state do not need to learn about the eating habits from New Delhi or Nagpur

 toornament main bharat ke alaava australia, south africa, srilanka or westeindies ke purv khilaadi apane jalwe dikhaaenge
 The tournament, which runs from 2–16 February in India, will feature several well-known former cricketers including Sachin Tendulkar, Brian Lara, Virender Sehwag, Brett Lee, Tillakaratne Dilshan and Jonty Rhodes
 46 varshiya tendulkar, test or vanade international main vishwa ke agrani scorer hai, jinhone 24 saal ke antarrashtriya kariyar main 34,000 se adhik ran banaae hai
 Which includes his 100 centuries
 bisisiai ne haal hi main is toornament ko bharat main karwaane kii manjuuri de di he

 During the Lok Sabha elections, former Uttar Pradesh Chief Minister and Samajwaji Party chief Akhilesh Yadav spoke to Aaj Tak openly on various issues
 super exclusive intervyuu main akhilesh yadav ne centre kii bijepi sarkaar or pradhanmantri narendra modi par nishaanaa to saadhaa hi, lekin vah congress ko bhi aade haathon lene se nahin chuke
 The SP chief said that Congress and BJP are the same
 congress mahasachiv priyanka gandhi wadra ke upi main mahagathbandhan ko madad pahunchane ke bayaan par akhilesh yadav ne kaha ki vah kanphyus hai jabaki congress adhyaksh rahul gandhi bhi virodhibhasi bayaan de rahe hai
